# A6: Indexes, triggers, user functions, transactions and population (Collaborative News)

Our product is called NewsLab. It consists of a collaborative news web application where anyone has the freedom to write and develop news about various topics and read about occurrences all around the world, serving as a platform not only to increase each one's awareness and knowledge about the world but also as a way to unite people and increase communication. It will be designed to create an all-encompassing place where people can write and discuss news in a collaborative manner, centralizing news and perspectives from all over the world allowing users to create a wholesome outlook on whatever subject they like.

In this artifact, various topics concerning the database and its access are addressed. 
First, some information was extracted and is shown, regarding the database workload. A table with the tuple ammount estimation can be seen in the first section. Still regarding this topic, the most frequent queries and updates to the database were also identified, and the correspondent SQL code generated.
Then, in another section of the artifact, the indexes, triggers, functions and transactions were identified. The full SQL script for the database (that contemplates not only the creation of the tables done in the last artifact, but also the previously mentioned topics) was written and is also presented in this section.
Finally, the SQL code for the database population is also presented, in the last section. The database was filled with test data, with an amount of tuples suitable for testing and with plausible values in each field.

## 1. Database Workload
 

 
### 1.1. Tuple Estimation
 

| **Relation reference** | **Relation Name** | **Order of magnitude** | **Estimated growth** |
| --- | ----------------- | ---------------------- | ---------------------|
| R01 | content           | hundreds of thousands  | thousands per day    |
| R02 | post              | tens of thousands      | hundreds per week    |
| R03 | comment           | tens of thousands      | hundreds per day     |
| R04 | reply             | tens of thousands      | hundreds per day     |
| R05 | user              | tens of thousands      | dozens per day       |
| R06 | admin             | dozens                 | little to no growth  |
| R07 | ban               | thousands              | units/dozens per day |
| R08 | badge             | 7                      | no growth            |
| R09 | notification      | thousands              | dozens per day       |
| R10 | location          | hundreds               | little to no growth  |
| R11 | country           | dozens                 | little to no growth  |
| R12 | report            | thousands              | dozens per day       |
| R13 | user_report       | hundreds               | dozens per day       |
| R14 | content_report    | hundreds               | dozens per day       |
| R15 | tag_report        | units                  | units per day        |
| R16 | reason            | 6                      | no growth            |
| R17 | tag               | dozens                 | units per day        |
| R18 | rating            | hundreds of thousands  | hundreds per day     |
| R19 | user_subscription | tens of thousands      | hundreds per day     |
| R20 | has_badge         | tens of thousands      | units/dozens per day |
| R21 | report_reason     | thousands              | dozens per day       |
| R22 | tag_subscription  | thousands              | dozens per day       |
| R23 | saved_post        | tens of thousands      | dozens/hundreds per day  |
| R24 | post_tag          | tens of thousands      | hundreds per day     |
| R25 | post_version      | thousands              | dozens per day       |
| R26 | comment_version   | thousands              | dozens per day       |
| R27 | reply_version     | thousands              | dozens per day       |

### 1.2. Frequent Queries
 

| **Query**       | SELECT01                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Selecting a specific post, having its ID |
| **Frequency**   | thousands per day                      |
| **SQL code**    | ``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id``` <br> ```FROM "content" c inner join post p on c.id = p.content_id ``` <br> ```WHERE c.id = $post_id; ``` |

| **Query**       | SELECT02                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Extracting the information of a specific post's author |
| **Frequency**   | thousands per day                      |
| **SQL code**    | ``` SELECT u.name, u.bio, u.verified, u.photo, l.name as city_name, c.name as country_name ``` <br> ```FROM "user" u inner join "location" l on u.location_id = l.id inner join country c on l.country_id = c.id``` <br> ```WHERE u.id = $author_id; ``` |


| **Query**       | SELECT03                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Extracting the tags of a specific post |
| **Frequency**   | thousands per day              |
| **SQL code**    | ``` SELECT t.id, t.name ``` <br> ```FROM tag t inner join post_tag pt on t.id = pt.tag_id ``` <br> ```WHERE pt.post_id = $post_id; ``` |


| **Query**       | SELECT04                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Extracting the comments of a post      |
| **Frequency**   | thousands per day              |
| **SQL code**    | ``` SELECT cm.content_id, c.body, c.likes_difference, cm.publication_date, cm.modification_date, u.name, u.photo, u.verified ``` <br> ```FROM "content" c inner join "comment" cm on c.id = cm.content_id inner join "user" u on c.author_id = u.id``` <br> ```WHERE cm.post_id = $post_id and c.most_recent = TRUE;``` |


| **Query**       | SELECT05                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Extracting the replies of a comment    |
| **Frequency**   | thousands per day          |
| **SQL code**    | ``` SELECT c.body, c.likes_difference, r.publication_date, r.modification_date, u.name, u.photo, u.verified ``` <br> ```FROM "content" c inner join reply r on c.id = r.content_id inner join "user" u on c.author_id = u.id``` <br> ```WHERE r.comment_id = $comment_id and c.most_recent = TRUE;```|


| **Query**       | SELECT06                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | User profile information   |
| **Frequency**   | hundreds per day          |
| **SQL code**    | _User Info_ <br>``` SELECT u.name, u.email, u.bio, u.birthday, u.verified, u.photo, l.name as city_name, c.name as country_name ``` <br> ```FROM "user" u inner join "location" l on u.location_id = l.id inner join country c on l.country_id = c.id``` <br> ```WHERE u.id = $user_id; ``` <br><br>_Number of Subs_<br> ``` SELECT count(distinct u.subscribing_user_id) as n_subs``` <br> ```FROM user_subscription u ``` <br> ```WHERE u.subscribed_user_id = $user_id; ``` <br><br> _Tag Stats_<br>``` SELECT t."name" as tag, count(*) ``` <br> ```FROM post_tag pt inner join tag t on pt.tag_id = t.id inner join post p on pt.post_id = p.content_id inner join content c on p.content_id = c.id``` <br> ```WHERE c.author_id = $user_id and c.most_recent = TRUE``` <br> ``` GROUP BY t."name"; ``` <br><br> _User Posts_<br> ``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo ``` <br> ```FROM "content" c inner join post p on c.id = p.content_id ``` <br> ```WHERE c.author_id = $user_id and c.most_recent = TRUE; ``` <br><br> _User Liked Posts_ <br> ``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id ``` <br> ``` FROM "content" c inner join post p on c.id = p.content_id inner join rating r on r.content_id = c.id``` <br> ```WHERE r.user_id = $user_id AND r.like = TRUE AND p.visible = TRUE;```<br><br> _User Liked Comments_ <br> ```SELECT cm.content_id as id, c.body, c.likes_difference, cm.publication_date as pub_date, cm.modification_date as mod_date, u.name as author, u.photo, u.verified, p.title as post_title, p.publication_date as post_pub_date, p.modification_date as post_mod_date, p.visible as post_visibility``` <br>```FROM "content" c inner join "comment" cm on c.id = cm.content_id inner join rating r on r.content_id = c.id inner join "user" u on c.author_id = u.id inner join post p on p.content_id = cm.post_id ``` <br> ```WHERE r.user_id = $user_id AND r.like = TRUE and c.most_recent = TRUE``` <br> ```UNION ``` <br>```SELECT rp.content_id as id, c.body, c.likes_difference, rp.publication_date as pub_date, rp.modification_date as mod_date, u.name as author, u.photo, u.verified,p.title as post_title, p.publication_date as post_pub_date, p.modification_date as post_mod_date, p.visible as post_visibility```<br>```FROM "content" c inner join reply rp on c.id = rp.content_id inner join rating r on r.content_id = c.id inner join "user" u on c.author_id = u.id inner join "comment" cm on cm.content_id = rp.comment_id inner join post p on p.content_id = cm.post_id```<br>```WHERE r.user_id = $user_id AND r.like = TRUE and c.most_recent = TRUE; ``` <br><br> _User Comments_<br> ```SELECT cm.content_id, c.body, c.likes_difference, cm.publication_date, cm.modification_date, p.title``` <br> ``` FROM "content" c inner join comment cm on c.id = cm.content_id inner join post p on cm.post_id = p.content_id ``` <br> ```WHERE c.author_id = $user_id and c.most_recent = TRUE ``` <br>```UNION```<br>```SELECT rp.content_id, c.body, c.likes_difference, rp.publication_date, rp.modification_date, p.title``` <br> ```FROM "content" c inner join reply rp on c.id = rp.content_id inner join "comment" cm on cm.content_id = rp.comment_id inner join post p on cm.post_id = p.content_id```<br> ```WHERE c.author_id = $user_id and c.most_recent = TRUE;```<br><br>_User Badges_ <br> ```SELECT b.icon, b.name, b.description``` <br> ``` FROM badge b inner join has_badge hb on b.id = hb.badge_id ``` <br> ```WHERE hb.user_id = $user_id; ``` |


| **Query**       | SELECT07                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Saved posts of a user    |
| **Frequency**   | dozens per day          |
| **SQL code**    | ```SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id``` <br> ```FROM "content" c inner join post p on c.id = p.content_id inner join saved_post sv on sv.post_id = c.id``` <br> ```WHERE sv.user_id = $user_id; ``` |

| **Query**       | SELECT08                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Get all pending notifications for a user |
| **Frequency**   | thousands per day          |
| **SQL code**    | ``` SELECT n.text, n.icon, n.domain, n."date" ``` <br> ```FROM "notification" n ``` <br> ```WHERE n.user_id = $user_id; ``` |

| **Query**       | SELECT09                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Get all the subscriptions (tags and authors) of a user    |
| **Frequency**   | hundreds a day          |
| **SQL code**    | _Tag Subscriptions_<br>``` SELECT t.name ``` <br> ```FROM tag t inner join tag_subscription ts on t.id = ts.tag_id``` <br> ```WHERE ts.user_id = $user_id; ``` <br><br> _User Subscriptions_ <br>``` SELECT u.name, u.email, u.photo, u.verified ``` <br> ```FROM "user" u inner join user_subscription us on u.id = us.subscribed_user_id``` <br> ```WHERE us.subscribing_user_id = $user_id; ``` |

| **Query**       | SELECT10                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Get previous versions of posts and comments/replies   |
| **Frequency**   | dozens a day          |
| **SQL code**    | _Post Version_ <br>``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id ``` <br> ```FROM post p inner join content c on p.content_id = c.id inner join post_version pv on pv.past_version_id = p.content_id``` <br> ``` WHERE pv.cur_version_id = $post_id; ``` <br><br> _Comment Version_<br> ``` SELECT cm.content_id, c.body, c.likes_difference, cm.publication_date, cm.modification_date, u.name, u.photo, u.verified ``` <br> ```FROM comment cm inner join content c on cm.content_id = c.id inner join "user" u on c.author_id = u.id inner join comment_version cv on cv.past_version_id = cm.content_id``` <br> ```WHERE cv.cur_version_id = $comment_id; ``` <br><br> _Reply Version_<br>``` SELECT r.content_id, c.body, c.likes_difference, r.publication_date, r.modification_date, u.name, u.photo, u.verified ``` <br> ```FROM reply r inner join content c on r.content_id = c.id inner join "user" u on c.author_id = u.id inner join reply_version rv on rv.past_version_id = r.content_id``` <br> ```WHERE rv.cur_version_id = $reply_id; ``` |

| **Query**       | SELECT11                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Select only posts that are news/opinions   |
| **Frequency**   | thousands a day          |
| **SQL code**    | _News_<br>``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id ``` <br> ```FROM post p inner join content c on p.content_id = c.id``` <br> ``` WHERE p.type = 'News' and c.most_recent = TRUE; ``` <br><br> _Opinion_<br>``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id ``` <br> ```FROM post p inner join content c on p.content_id = c.id``` <br> ``` WHERE p.type = 'Opinion' and c.most_recent = TRUE; ```  |

| **Query**       | SELECT12                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Select some popular/hot posts and tags (ex: in the last month)   |
| **Frequency**   | hundreds/thousands a day          |
| **SQL code**    | _Posts_<br>``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id ``` <br> ```FROM post p inner join content c on p.content_id = c.id``` <br> ``` WHERE date_part('day',now()- p.publication_date) < 30 and c.most_recent = TRUE and p.visible = TRUE``` <br> ```ORDER BY c.likes_difference DESC``` <br> ```LIMIT $num_posts; ``` <br><br> _Tags_<br>``` SELECT t.name, sum(c.likes_difference) as sum_likes``` <br> ```FROM tag t inner join post_tag pt on t.id = pt.tag_id inner join post p on p.content_id = pt.post_id inner join content c on p.content_id = c.id ``` <br> ``` WHERE date_part('day',now()- p.publication_date) < 30 and c.most_recent = TRUE and p.visible = TRUE``` <br> ```GROUP BY t.name ``` <br> ```ORDER BY sum_likes DESC``` <br> ```LIMIT $num_tags; ``` |

| **Query**       | SELECT13                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Select the latest posts   |
| **Frequency**   | thousands a day          |
| **SQL code**    | ``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id  ``` <br> ```FROM post p inner join content c on p.content_id = c.id``` <br> ```WHERE p.visible = TRUE and c.most_recent = TRUE``` <br> ```ORDER BY p.publication_date DESC; ``` |

| **Query**       | SELECT14                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Select posts of a given tag  |
| **Frequency**   | thousands per day          |
| **SQL code**    | _News_<br>``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id ``` <br> ```FROM post p inner join content c on p.content_id = c.id inner join post_tag pt on pt.post_id = p.content_id ``` <br> ```WHERE pt.tag_id = $tag_id AND p.type = 'News' AND p.visible = TRUE AND c.most_recent = TRUE; ``` <br><br> _Opinion_<br>``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, c.author_id ``` <br> ```FROM post p inner join content c on p.content_id = c.id inner join post_tag pt on pt.post_id = p.content_id ``` <br> ```WHERE pt.tag_id = $tag_id AND p.type = 'Opinion' AND p.visible = TRUE AND c.most_recent = TRUE; ``` |


| **Query**       | SELECT15                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Information for the admin center page   |
| **Frequency**   | units/dozens per day          |
| **SQL code**    | _General Info_<br>``` SELECT u.name, u.email, u.birthday, u.photo, l.name, c.name, a.posts_deleted, a.comments_deleted, a.reports_solved, a.users_banned ``` <br> ```FROM "user" u inner join "location" l on u.location_id = l.id inner join country c on l.country_id = c.id inner join "admin" a on u.id = a.user_id``` <br> ```WHERE a.user_id = $admin_id; ``` <br><br> _Admin List_<br>``` SELECT u.name, u.email, a.posts_deleted, a.comments_deleted, a.reports_solved, a.users_banned ``` <br> ```FROM "user" u inner join "admin" a on u.id = a.user_id;``` <br><br>_Report List_<br>``` SELECT r.explanation, r.reporter_id, u.name, ur.user_id, cr.content_id, tr.tag_id, r.closed ``` <br> ```FROM "user" u inner join report r on r.reporter_id = u.id left join user_report ur on r.id = ur.report_id left join content_report cr on r.id = cr.report_id left join tag_report tr on r.id = tr.report_id;``` <br><br> _Ban List_<br>``` SELECT ub.name as banned_user, ua.name as admin_name, b.ban_start, b.ban_end ``` <br> ``` FROM "user" ub inner join ban b on ub.id = b.user_id inner join "user" ua on b.admin_id = ua.id;```|


| **Query**       | SELECT16                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Filter and search for specific content |
| **Frequency**   | thousands per day     |
| **SQL code**    | _Search for news_ <br>``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, u.name, rank ``` <br> ```FROM "content" c inner join post p on c.id = p.content_id inner join "user" u on c.author_id = u.id,``` <br> ```  ts_rank_cd(setweight(to_tsvector('simple', p.title), 'A') \|\| ' ' \|\| setweight(to_tsvector('simple', c.body), 'B') \|\| ' ' \|\| setweight(to_tsvector('simple', u.name), 'D'), plainto_tsquery('simple', $search_str)) as rank``` <br> ``` WHERE p.type = 'News' AND p.visible = TRUE AND c.most_recent = TRUE AND rank > 0 ``` <br> ```ORDER BY rank DESC;``` <br><br> _Search for opinions_ <br>``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.visible, p.type, p.photo, u.name, rank ``` <br> ```FROM "content" c inner join post p on c.id = p.content_id inner join "user" u on c.author_id = u.id,``` <br> ``` ts_rank_cd(setweight(to_tsvector('simple', p.title), 'A') \|\| ' ' \|\| setweight(to_tsvector('simple', c.body), 'B') \|\| ' ' \|\| setweight(to_tsvector('simple', u.name), 'D'), plainto_tsquery('simple', $search_str)) as rank``` <br> ``` WHERE p.type = 'Opinion' AND p.visible = TRUE AND c.most_recent = TRUE AND rank > 0 ``` <br> ```ORDER BY rank DESC;```  <br><br> _Search for authors/users_ <br>``` SELECT u.name, u.verified, u.photo, u.email, rank ``` <br> ```FROM "user" u, ts_rank_cd(to_tsvector(u.name), plainto_tsquery('simple', $search_str)) as rank``` <br> ```WHERE rank > 0 ``` <br> ```ORDER BY rank DESC;``` <br><br> _Search for tags_ <br>``` SELECT t."name", rank ``` <br>``` FROM tag t, ts_rank_cd(to_tsvector(t."name"), plainto_tsquery('simple', $search_str)) as rank ``` <br> ``` WHERE rank > 0 ``` <br> ```ORDER BY rank DESC;``` |

| **Query**       | SELECT17                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Query user information to perform login operation   |
| **Frequency**   | thousands per day          |
| **SQL code**    | ``` SELECT u.email, u.password ``` <br> ```FROM "user" u``` <br> ```WHERE u.email = $email;``` |

| **Query**       | SELECT18                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Query user posts                       |
| **Frequency**   | hundreds/thousands per day          |
| **SQL code**    | ``` SELECT p.title, c.body, p.publication_date, p.modification_date, c.likes_difference, p.type, p.photo ``` <br> ```FROM "content" c inner join post p on c.id = p.content_id``` <br> ```WHERE c.author_id = $user_id and c.most_recent = TRUE and p.visible = TRUE; ``` |


### 1.3. Frequent Updates


| **Query**       | INSERT01                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Sign up new user  |
| **Frequency**   | dozens per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO "user" (email, name, birthday, password) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($email, $name, $birthday, $password);``` |

| **Query**       | INSERT02                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | New post  |
| **Frequency**   | hundreds per week                     |
| **SQL code**    | ```-- if post is published immediately``` <br> ```INSERT INTO "content" (body, author_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($body, $user_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO post (content_id, title, visible, type, photo) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($content_id, $title, $visible, $type, $photo);``` <br><br> ```-- if post was scheduled``` <br> ``` INSERT INTO "content" (body, author_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($body, $user_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO post (content_id, title, publication_date, visible, type, photo) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($content_id, $title, $publication_date, $visible, $type, $photo);``` |

| **Query**       | INSERT03                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | New comment / reply  |
| **Frequency**   | hundreds per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO "content" (body, author_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($body, $user_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO "comment" (content_id, post_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($content_id, $post_id);``` <br><br><br> ``` INSERT INTO "content" (body, author_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($body, $user_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO reply (content_id, comment_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($content_id, $comment_id);``` |

| **Query**       | INSERT04                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | New like/dislike on content  |
| **Frequency**   | hundreds per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO rating (content_id, user_id, "like") ``` <br> ```VALUES ($content_id, $user_id, $like);``` |

| **Query**       | INSERT05                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | New subscription (user or tag)  |
| **Frequency**   | hundreds per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO user_subscription (subscribing_user_id, subscribed_user_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($user_id, $subscribed_user_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO tag_subscription (user_id, tag_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($user_id, $tag_id);```|

| **Query**       | INSERT06                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | New notification for user  |
| **Frequency**   | hundreds per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO "notification" ("text", icon, domain, user_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($text, $icon, $domain, $user_id);``` |

| **Query**       | INSERT07                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | User earns new badge  |
| **Frequency**   | units/dozens per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO has_badge (user_id, badge_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($user_id, $badge_id);``` |

| **Query**       | INSERT08                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | User reports a user, content or tag  |
| **Frequency**   | units/dozens per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO report (explanation, reporter_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($explanation, $user_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO report_reason (report_id, reason_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($report_id, $reason_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO user_report (report_id, user_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($report_id, $user_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO content_report (report_id, content_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($report_id, $content_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO tag_report (report_id, tag_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($report_id, $tag_id);``` |

| **Query**       | INSERT09                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Admin bans a user  |
| **Frequency**   | units/dozens per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO ban (ban_start, ban_end, user_id, admin_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($ban_start, $ban_end, $user_id, $admin_id);``` |

| **Query**       | INSERT10                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | User saves a post  |
| **Frequency**   | dozens/hundreds per day                |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO saved_post (user_id, post_id) ``` <br> ```VALUES ($user_id, $post_id);``` |

| **Query**       | INSERT11                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Inserting a new admin                  |
| **Frequency**   | units per month                        |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO "admin" (user_id) ``` <br>```VALUES ($user_id);```|

| **Query**       | INSERT12                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Insert a new tag                       |
| **Frequency**   | units per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO tag ("name") ``` <br>```VALUES ($name);```|

| **Query**       | INSERT13                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Insert a new post/comment/reply version |
| **Frequency**   | dozens per day                     |
| **SQL code**    | ``` INSERT INTO post_version (past_version_id, cur_version_id) ``` <br>```VALUES ($past_version_id, $cur_version_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO comment_version (past_version_id, cur_version_id) ``` <br>```VALUES ($past_version_id, $cur_version_id);``` <br><br> ``` INSERT INTO reply_version (past_version_id, cur_version_id) ``` <br>```VALUES ($past_version_id, $cur_version_id);```|

-----------

| **Query**       | UPDATE01                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |
| **Description** | Update user information                |
| **Frequency**   | units/dozens per day                   |
| **SQL code**    | ``` UPDATE "user"``` <br> ``` SET email = $email, name = $name, password = $password, bio = $bio, birthday = $birthday, location_id = $location_id, photo = $photo ``` <br>```WHERE id = $user_id;```|

| **Query**       | UPDATE05                               |
| ---             | ---                                    |

| **Frequency**   | dozens per day                         |
| **SQL code**    | ``` UPDATE rating``` <br> ``` SET "like" = $like ``` <br>```WHERE content_id = $content_id AND user_id = $user_id;```|

## 2. Proposed Indices

### 2.1. Performance Indices

**NOTE**: Because we using version 9 of PostgreSQL, hash indexes are not available. Therefore, in this document, when a hash index is specified, what will be actually used is a B-Tree index.


| **Index**           | ID01                                   |
| ---                 | ---                                    |
| **Related queries** | SELECT06, SELECT18, TRIGGER07, TRIGGER04 |
| **Relation**        | content                                |
| **Attribute**       | author_id                              |
| **Type**            | Hash                                   |
| **Cardinality**     | Medium                                 |
| **Clustering**      | Yes                                    |
| **Justification**   | Queries that search for posts/comments/replies/content of a given user are used often and need to be fast. We don't need range search nor sorting. User's may have a fair ammount of posts/comments/replies/content. Since we need to fetch all posts/comments/replies/content of the user and it's cardinality is medium, clustering would increase performance.   |
| **SQL code**        | ``` CREATE INDEX content_author ON "content" USING hash (author_id); ```                                      |

| **Index**           | ID02                                   |
| ---                 | ---                                    |
| **Related queries** | SELECT10                               |
| **Relation**        | post_version                           |
| **Attribute**       | cur_version_id                         |
| **Type**            | Hash                                   |
| **Cardinality**     | Medium                                 |
| **Clustering**      | Yes                                    |
| **Justification**   | Getting the previous versions of a post doesn't require range selecting nor sorting. A post may have multiple versions and having clustering would decrease the number of blocks needed to be fetched due to queries.   |
| **SQL code**        |       ``` CREATE INDEX post_versions ON post_version USING hash (cur_version_id); ```                                     |

| **Index**           | ID03                                   |
| ---                 | ---                                    |
| **Related queries** | SELECT10                               |
| **Relation**        | comment_version                        |
| **Attribute**       | cur_version_id                         |
| **Type**            | Hash                                   |
| **Cardinality**     | Medium                                 |
| **Clustering**      | Yes                                    |
| **Justification**   | Getting the previous versions of a comment doesn't require range selecting nor sorting. A comment may have multiple versions and having clustering would decrease the number of blocks needed to be fetched due to queries.   |
| **SQL code**        | ``` CREATE INDEX comment_versions ON "comment_version" USING hash (cur_version_id); ```                                           |

| **Index**           | ID04                                   |
| ---                 | ---                                    |
| **Related queries** | SELECT10                               |
| **Relation**        | reply_version                          |
| **Attribute**       | cur_version_id                         |
| **Type**            | Hash                                   |
| **Cardinality**     | Medium                                 |
| **Clustering**      | Yes                                    |
| **Justification**   | Getting the previous versions of a reply doesn't require range selecting nor sorting. A reply may have multiple versions and having clustering would decrease the number of blocks needed to be fetched due to queries.   |
| **SQL code**        |      ``` CREATE INDEX reply_versions ON "reply_version" USING hash (cur_version_id); ```                                        |

| **Index**           | ID05                                   |
| ---                 | ---                                    |
| **Related queries** | SELECT12, SELECT13                     |
| **Relation**        | post                           |
| **Attribute**       | publication_date                         |
| **Type**            | B-Tree                                   |
| **Cardinality**     | Medium                                 |
| **Clustering**      | No                                    |
| **Justification**   | Presenting trending posts and search results imply the need of sorting and fetching them by range. As such we chose to use B-Tree indexes. To aid the quick range fetching, we don't use clustering |
| **SQL code**        |       ``` CREATE INDEX post_dates ON post USING btree (publication_date); ```                                       |

### 2.2. Full-text Search Indices 

| **Index**           | ID06                                   |
| ---                 | ---                                    |
| **Related queries** | SELECT16                          |
| **Relation**        | post    |
| **Attribute**       | search  |
| **Type**            | GIST              |
| **Clustering**      | No                |
| **Justification**   | To speed up the searching process for posts. As the 'search' field on a post depends on its title, body and author's name, GiST is used because those fields may be changed rather frequently (specially the title and body), and GiST is better for dynamic data and faster for updates.  |
| **SQL code**        | ``` CREATE INDEX post_search_idx ON post USING GIST (search); ``` |

| **Index**           | ID07                                   |
| ---                 | ---                                    |
| **Related queries** | SELECT16                          |
| **Relation**        | user    |
| **Attribute**       | search   |
| **Type**            | GIST              |
| **Clustering**      | No                |
| **Justification**   | To speed up the searching process for users (through their name). GiST is used because the name of a user may be changed (although not very frequently), and GiST is better for dynamic data and faster for updates.   |
| **SQL code**        | ``` CREATE INDEX user_search_idx ON "user" USING GIST (search); ```                                     |

| **Index**           | ID08                                   |
| ---                 | ---                                    |
| **Related queries** | SELECT16                          |
| **Relation**        | tag    |
| **Attribute**       | search   |
| **Type**            | GIN                            |
| **Clustering**      | No                |
| **Justification**   | To speed up the searching process for tags (through their name). GIN is used because the name of a tag is not changed, and this type of index is better/faster for static data.   |
| **SQL code**        | ``` CREATE INDEX tag_search_idx ON tag USING GIN (search); ```           |

## 3. Triggers & UDF

### 3.1 Triggers

| **Trigger**      | TRIGGER01                              |
| ---              | ---                                    |
| **Description**  | Trigger that connects the different versions of a post/comment/reply  (connected to **BR12: Edited tag**) |
 **SQL code**   

``` sql
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION content_latest_version() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$
DECLARE
    cid bigint;
    tuple RECORD;
    row RECORD;
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO "content" (body, most_recent, likes_difference, author_id) VALUES (OLD.body, FALSE, OLD.likes_difference, OLD.author_id) RETURNING "id" INTO cid;

    IF OLD.id IN (SELECT content_ID FROM post)
    THEN
        SELECT * INTO tuple FROM post WHERE content_id = OLD.id;

        INSERT INTO post VALUES (
            cid, tuple.title, tuple.publication_date, tuple.modification_date, tuple.visible, tuple.type, tuple.photo
        );

        INSERT INTO post_version VALUES(cid, OLD.id);

        FOR row IN SELECT * FROM post_tag WHERE post_id = OLD.id
        LOOP
            INSERT INTO post_tag VALUES (cid, row.tag_id);
        END LOOP;

    ELSEIF OLD.id IN (SELECT content_ID FROM "comment")
    THEN
        SELECT * INTO tuple FROM "comment" WHERE content_id = OLD.id;

        INSERT INTO "comment" VALUES (
            cid, tuple.publication_date, tuple.modification_date, tuple.post_id
        );

        UPDATE "comment" SET modification_date = now() WHERE content_id = OLD.id;

        INSERT INTO comment_version VALUES(cid, OLD.id);

    ELSEIF OLD.id IN (SELECT content_id FROM reply)
    THEN
        SELECT * INTO tuple FROM reply WHERE content_id = OLD.id;

        INSERT INTO "reply" VALUES (
            cid, tuple.publication_date, tuple.modification_date, tuple.comment_id
        );

        UPDATE "reply" SET modification_date = now() WHERE content_id = OLD.id;

        INSERT INTO comment_version VALUES(cid, OLD.id);
    END IF;

    RETURN NEW;
END;
$BODY$
LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS content_latest_version ON "content";
CREATE TRIGGER content_latest_version
    BEFORE UPDATE OF body ON "content"
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE content_latest_version();

```

| **Trigger**      | TRIGGER02                              |
| ---              | ---                                    |
| **Description**  | Update an admin's statistics accordingly |

**SQL code**   


``` sql

-- Reports solved statistic

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION upd_admin_reports_solved() RETURNS TRIGGER AS $BODY$ <br> BEGIN
    UPDATE "admin" SET reports_solved = reports_solved + 1 WHERE NEW.solver_id = user_id;

    RETURN NEW;
END
$BODY$

LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS update_admin_reports_solved_on_update ON report;
CREATE TRIGGER update_admin_reports_solved_on_update
    BEFORE UPDATE ON report
    FOR EACH ROW
    WHEN (NEW.solver_id IS NOT NULL and NEW.solver_id != OLD.solver_id)
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE upd_admin_reports_solved();

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS update_admin_reports_solved_on_insert ON report;
CREATE TRIGGER update_admin_reports_solved_on_insert
    BEFORE INSERT ON report
    FOR EACH ROW
    WHEN (NEW.solver_id IS NOT NULL) 
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE upd_admin_reports_solved();    

-- Users banned statistics

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION upd_admin_users_banned() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

BEGIN

    UPDATE "admin" SET users_banned = users_banned + 1 WHERE user_id = NEW.admin_id;

    RETURN NULL;
END
$BODY$

LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS update_admin_users_banned ON ban;
CREATE TRIGGER update_admin_users_banned
    AFTER INSERT ON ban
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE upd_admin_users_banned();
``` 


| **Trigger**      | TRIGGER03                              |
| ---              | ---                                    |
| **Description**  | Update a user's banned status after an admin establishes a ban for him  |

**SQL code** 


``` sql
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION upd_user_banned_status() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

BEGIN

    IF NEW.ban_end is NULL or NEW.ban_end > now() THEN
        UPDATE "user" SET banned = TRUE WHERE id = NEW.user_id;
    ELSE
        UPDATE "user" SET banned = FALSE WHERE id = NEW.user_id;
    END IF;

    RETURN NULL;
END
$BODY$

LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS update_user_banned_status ON ban;
CREATE TRIGGER update_user_banned_status
    AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE ON ban
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE upd_user_banned_status();
```

| **Trigger**      | TRIGGER04                              |
| ---              | ---                                    |
| **Description**  | Update the likes difference of a content when a user likes/dislikes (also prevents a user from liking/disliking his/her own content (connected to **BR08: self-vote**)) |
**SQL code**   

``` sql
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION upd_rating_on_insert() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

BEGIN

    IF EXISTS (SELECT * FROM content WHERE id = NEW.content_id and author_id = NEW.user_id) THEN

        RAISE EXCEPTION 'User can give itself a rating';

    END IF;

    IF NEW."like" = TRUE THEN
        UPDATE content SET likes_difference = likes_difference + 1 WHERE id = NEW.content_id;
    ELSE
        UPDATE content SET likes_difference = likes_difference - 1 WHERE id = NEW.content_id;
    END IF;

    RETURN NEW;

END

$BODY$
LANGUAGE plpgsql;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION upd_rating_on_update() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

BEGIN

    IF EXISTS (SELECT * FROM content WHERE id = NEW.content_id and author_id = NEW.user_id) THEN

        RAISE EXCEPTION 'User can give itself a rating';
    END IF;
    -- Remove old rating
    IF OLD."like" = TRUE THEN
        UPDATE content SET likes_difference = likes_difference - 1 WHERE id = NEW.content_id;

    ELSE
        UPDATE content SET likes_difference = likes_difference + 1 WHERE id = NEW.content_id;

    END IF;

    -- Add new rating
    IF NEW."like" = TRUE THEN
        UPDATE content SET likes_difference = likes_difference + 1 WHERE id = NEW.content_id;
    ELSE
        UPDATE content SET likes_difference = likes_difference - 1 WHERE id = NEW.content_id;
    END IF;

    RETURN NEW;

END

$BODY$
LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS update_rating_on_insert ON rating;
CREATE TRIGGER update_rating_on_insert
    BEFORE INSERT ON rating
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE upd_rating_on_insert();

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS update_rating_on_update ON rating;
CREATE TRIGGER update_rating_on_update
    BEFORE UPDATE ON rating
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE upd_rating_on_update();


```


| **Trigger**      | TRIGGER05                              |
| ---              | ---                                    |
| **Description**  | Prevent a user from reporting himself (connected to **BR09: self-report**) |

**SQL code**   
``` sql
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION chck_self_report() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

DECLARE
    reporter INTEGER;

BEGIN

    SELECT reporter_id INTO reporter FROM report WHERE id = NEW.report_id;

    IF reporter = NEW.user_id THEN
        RAISE EXCEPTION 'Cannot report self';
    END IF;

    RETURN NEW;
END
$BODY$

LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS check_self_report ON user_report;
CREATE TRIGGER check_self_report
    BEFORE INSERT ON user_report 
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE chck_self_report();

```

| **Trigger**      | TRIGGER06                              |
| ---              | ---                                    |
| **Description**  | Update a user's verified status, if he all badges (and therefore has the 'Verified' badge)  (connected to **BR01: verified users**)|
**SQL code**   


``` sql
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_user_verified() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$
DECLARE
    total_badges bigint;
    user_badges bigint;
BEGIN
    SELECT COUNT(badge_id) INTO user_badges
    FROM has_badge hb INNER JOIN
         badge b ON b.id = hb.badge_id
    WHERE hb.user_id = NEW.user_id AND b.name != 'Verified';

    SELECT COUNT("id") INTO total_badges
    FROM badge
    WHERE badge.name != 'Verified';

    IF user_badges = total_badges
    THEN
        UPDATE "user" SET verified = TRUE WHERE id = NEW.user_id;
        INSERT INTO has_badge (user_id, badge_id) VALUES (NEW.user_id, 1);
    END IF;

    RETURN NEW;
END
$BODY$
LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS trigger_update_user_verified ON has_badge;
CREATE TRIGGER trigger_update_user_verified
    AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE ON has_badge
    FOR EACH ROW
    WHEN (NEW.badge_id != 1)
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE update_user_verified();
```

| **Trigger**      | TRIGGER07                              |
| ---              | ---                                    |
| **Description**  | Give a user a certain badge if its corresponding event occurs |
**SQL code**   


``` sql
-- TAG MASTER 

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION give_badge_tag_master() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$
DECLARE
    author bigint;
BEGIN
    SELECT author_id INTO author FROM content WHERE content.id = NEW.content_id;

    IF (SELECT COUNT (DISTINCT post_tag.tag_id)
        FROM content INNER JOIN
             post ON content.id = post.content_id INNER JOIN
             post_tag ON content_id = post_tag.post_id
        WHERE content.author_id = author AND content.most_recent = TRUE) >= 10
    THEN
        INSERT INTO has_badge VALUES (author, 7);
    END IF;
    RETURN NULL;
END
$BODY$
LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS trigger_give_badge_tag_master ON post_tag;
CREATE TRIGGER trigger_give_badge_tag_master
    AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE ON post_tag
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE PROCEDURE give_badge_tag_master();

``` 

```sql
-- POPULAR BADGE

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION give_badge_popular() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

DECLARE
  sub_count INTEGER;
  bdge_id INTEGER;

BEGIN

    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO sub_count FROM user_subscription WHERE subscribed_user_id = NEW.subscribed_user_id;
    SELECT id INTO bdge_id FROM badge WHERE name = 'Popular' ;

    IF sub_count >= 100 THEN
       INSERT INTO has_badge (user_id,badge_id) VALUES (NEW.subscribed_user_id,bdge_id);
    END IF;

    RETURN NULL;
END
$BODY$

LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS give_badge_popular ON user_subscription;
CREATE TRIGGER give_badge_popular
    AFTER INSERT ON user_subscription 
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE give_badge_popular();
    
``` 

``` sql

-- VIOLET BADGE

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION give_badge_violet() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

DECLARE

    authorid INTEGER;
    comment_count INTEGER;
    reply_count INTEGER;
    bdge_id INTEGER;

BEGIN

    SELECT c.author_id INTO authorid
    FROM "content" c inner join comment cm on c.id = cm.content_id
    WHERE cm.content_id = NEW.content_id;

    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO comment_count
    FROM "content" c inner join comment cm on c.id = cm.content_id
    WHERE c.author_id = authorid AND c.most_recent = TRUE;

    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO reply_count
    FROM "content" c inner join reply r on c.id = r.content_id
    WHERE c.author_id = authorid AND c.most_recent = TRUE;

    SELECT id INTO bdge_id FROM badge WHERE name = 'Violet' ;

    IF comment_count + reply_count >= 10 THEN
       INSERT INTO has_badge (user_id,badge_id) VALUES (authorid,bdge_id);

END
$BODY$

LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS give_badge_violet_comment ON comment;
CREATE TRIGGER give_badge_violet_comment
    AFTER INSERT ON comment 
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE give_badge_violet();

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS give_badge_violet_comment ON reply;
CREATE TRIGGER give_badge_violet_reply
    AFTER INSERT ON reply 
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE give_badge_violet();

```

```sql
-- TARGETED BADGE


CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION give_badge_targeted() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

DECLARE

    total_count INTEGER;
    authorid INTEGER;
    bdge_id INTEGER;

BEGIN

    SELECT c.author_id INTO authorid
    FROM (
            SELECT *
            FROM "content"
            WHERE id = NEW.content_id

    ) as c;


    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO total_count
    FROM
        (SELECT r.content_id as id
        FROM "content" c INNER JOIN reply r on c.id = r.content_id 
        WHERE c.most_recent = TRUE and r.comment_id in (SELECT cm.content_id 
                                                        FROM "content" c INNER JOIN "comment" cm on c.id = cm.content_id 
                                                        WHERE cm.post_id = 4 and c.most_recent = TRUE)

        UNION ALL

        (SELECT cm.content_id 
        FROM "content" c INNER JOIN "comment" cm on c.id = cm.content_id 
        WHERE cm.post_id = 4 and c.most_recent = TRUE)) as cnt;

    SELECT id INTO bdge_id FROM badge WHERE name = 'Targeted' ;

    IF total_count >= 10 THEN
       INSERT INTO has_badge (user_id,badge_id) VALUES (authorid,bdge_id);
    END IF;

    RETURN NULL;

END
$BODY$

LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS give_badge_targeted ON comment;
CREATE TRIGGER give_badge_targeted
    AFTER INSERT ON comment 
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE give_badge_targeted();

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS give_badge_targeted ON reply;
CREATE TRIGGER give_badge_targeted
    AFTER INSERT ON reply 
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE give_badge_targeted();

```

```sql
-- MR WORLDWIDE BADGE

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION give_badge_worldwide() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

DECLARE

    country_count INTEGER;
    badge_id INTEGER;

BEGIN

    SELECT count(DISTINCT c.name) INTO country_count
    FROM user_subscription sub  JOIN "user" u ON sub.subscribing_user_id = u.id 
                            JOIN "location" loc ON loc.id = u.location_id 
                            JOIN "country" c ON loc.country_id = c.id
    WHERE subscribed_user_id = NEW.subscribed_user_id

    SELECT id INTO badge_id FROM badge WHERE name = 'Mr WorldWide' ;

    IF country_count >= 10 THEN
       INSERT INTO has_badge (user_id,badge_id) VALUES (NEW.subscribed_user_id,badge_id);
    END IF;

    RETURN NULL;
END
$BODY$

LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS give_badge_worldwide ON user_subscription;
CREATE TRIGGER give_badge_worldwide
    AFTER INSERT ON user_subscription 
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE give_badge_worldwide();
```
```sql
-- CHAMPION BADGE
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION give_badge_champion() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$

DECLARE

    num_popular_articles INTEGER;
    badge_id INTEGER;

BEGIN
    -- if content is post 
    IF NEW.content_id IN (SELECT content_id FROM post) THEN
        -- get all posts of the user with 100+ likes
        SELECT count(c.id) INTO num_popular_articles
        FROM "content" c
        WHERE c.author_id = NEW.user_id AND (SELECT count(r.user_id) FROM rating r WHERE r.content_id = c.id) >= 100;

        IF num_popular_articles >= 5 THEN
            SELECT id INTO badge_id FROM badge WHERE name = 'Champion' ;
            INSERT INTO has_badge (user_id,badge_id) VALUES (NEW.user_id,badge_id);
        END IF;
    
    END IF;

    RETURN NULL;
END
$BODY$

LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS give_badge_champion ON rating;
CREATE TRIGGER give_badge_champion
    AFTER INSERT ON rating
    FOR EACH ROW
    WHEN (NEW."like" = TRUE)
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE give_badge_champion();
```

| **Trigger**      | TRIGGER08                              |

``` sql
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_modification_date() RETURNS TRIGGER AS
$BODY$
BEGIN
    NEW.modification_date = now();
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$BODY$
LANGUAGE plpgsql;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS post_modification_date ON post;
CREATE TRIGGER post_modification_date
    BEFORE UPDATE OF title, photo ON post
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE update_modification_date();
```

| **Trigger**      | TRIGGER09                              |
| ---              | ---                                    |
| **Description**  | Generate the search tsvector for the full text search on users|

**SQL code**

``` sql

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION user_search_update() RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    IF TG_OP = 'INSERT' THEN
        NEW.search = to_tsvector('simple', NEW.name);
    END IF;
    IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' THEN
        IF NEW.name <> OLD.name THEN
            NEW.search = to_tsvector('simple', NEW.name);
        END IF;
    END IF;
    RETURN NEW;
END
$$ LANGUAGE 'plpgsql';

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS user_search_update ON "user";
CREATE TRIGGER user_search_update
    BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON "user"
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE user_search_update();

```

    IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' THEN
